select t.TABLE_NAME || '|' ||
       s.COLUMN_NAME || '|' ||
       s.DATA_TYPE || '|' ||
	   s.DATA_LENGTH || '|' ||
	   s.DATA_PRECISION || '|' ||
	   t.NUM_ROWS
from DBA_TABLES t,DBA_TAB_COLUMNS s
where t.table_name = s.table_name
and   t.OWNER  = '&schema';
